 itane anubhav ke baad aapako pataa hota he ki filmein aati hai, or jaati hai

 in donon ne 12 april ko bharat ke hyderabad main shaadi kii thi
 Both reached Jinnah International Airport from Mumbai on Thursday
 yah joda guuruuvaar ko hi islamabad ke liye ravaanaa hoga, jahaan pakistan ke pradhanmantri yusuf raja gilaani or bhartiya ucchayeg ne unke liye resepshan yojit kiya he

 Mohammed Ali Shah was the only dignitary to meet the two comfortably

 Security personnel also prevented the media from getting close to the pair
 purv captain kapil dev ne kaha ki bhartiya ballebaaji ke mukhya sirmaur viraat kohli vishwa cricket main kisi anya cricketer se zyada record apane naam karenge

 i do not compare
 jaise doosraa don breadman nahin ho saktaa, usee tarah doosraa sachin tendulkar nahin ho saktaa

 11 such unnecessary English words that it would be wise to leave
